< Text>
One of Westchester's last Local Treasures.
This is a place thats been around forever and needs to stay around. Would you like that new album in CD or Vinyl? Want the classics they got you. Need a collectors item for a gift they got you.

Cd's,Cassettes, Dvd's, Vinyl, 45's, etc. They got it. Also tour and movie poster's, shirts, decals, one of a kind music items can be found here.
You can also sell/trade them cds,dvds, memorabilia, etc.

If you haven't been here, it's definitely a spot that folks should make their way to see if visiting LA.

Local Favorite. Small business. Community Staple. reaLA< /Text>

<user>117407545045910557407< /user><username>Amy Grace<//username><date>1361512296693</date><rating>5<//rating>< Review>
‚ÄúLong Live Rock n Roll‚Äù

In a digital era of downloadable tunes, it‚Äôs time to ask ourselves a deep question. Are we ready as a society to nail the coffin shut, burying our intangible memories when music had a soul, a voice, and a pictorial visualization?

Do you remember the feeling of giddiness and anticipation as we tore off that annoying cellophane‚Äîonly to unveil our favorite artist‚Äôs newest release we played loud and proud as we browsed through the vivid, artistic, & artist-inspired interpretation of their compilation as depicted through the cover art design and flip through the mysterious insert within?

I only ponder this thought because I made a recent CD purchase. (My last CD purchase, if memory serves me right, was the exact moment Vanilla Ice‚Äôs single, ‚ÄúICE ICE BABY‚Äù released.) [Feel free to stop reading for my honesty and embarrassment‚Äìwhich I why I will never put my name to this piece.]

As my taste buds for fine wine have with time acquired, so has my yearning for meaningful lyrics & varying artistic expressions of similar pains and torment I have experienced.

I bought Pearl Jam‚Äôs Greatest Hits, 1991-2003; again, no music-connoisseur by any means but my taste is slowly maturing. I held the cardboard dual CD case in awe only to unveil the poignant insert that for a brief time forced me to escape this reality I have created.

I sat paralyzed, flipping through the black & white pages depicting their early years as they built by hand the cover photo backdrop for their introductory album, ‚ÄúTEN‚Äù. Then, something happened. As I listened to the music I‚Äôve heard over and over in my past, I now listened with virgin ears. What changed? I now heard the feeling. It was a foreign experience that a mere CD insert imploded upon my senses. I heard pain, life, struggle, hardship, regret, love, tragedy, innocence, and human error. I saw myself in the ugliest of states on up to my greatest sense of strength.

I am humbled by this experience‚Ä¶enough to recount the event. If you‚Äôre seeking a conclusion, my best articulation is that convenience has stolen my youth.
I will never be able to pass on this feeling or experience to my baby girl. She will most likely never hold a CD cover or glimpse at an antiquated insert so as long as her iPhone or ‚Äòi-Whatever‚Äô consumes her life in 2027.

But I‚Äôll never forget.

Call it a plug, call it what you will. Keep local, low-budget radio stations & record stores funded; at least enough to light the dim road the strike a match to, unleashing the power that only music possesses.

In the end, I am however just a hopeless nostalgic and feel entitled to embellish. If you‚Äôre ever in LA, stop by Soundsations. I have visited the small record store merely twice, but they‚Äôve been such a significant presence in my life for well over a decade.</Review>

<text>This place gives good trade for cds, DVDs, blurays, vinyl and video games! The new stuff they carry always tend to be cheaper than buying even from eBay. However sometimes the used stuff they carry, they try to sell at new prices or near new prices. But I've also found some cool promo albums(industry only stuffs) as well as older hard to find stuff. There big downfall to me is that they are a small store with not enough inventory to meet my needs. They don't actively try to restock things that sell and would rather order a record for you. This may sound like a bunch of negative stuff but when you buy a new record for $10 cheaper than eBay, you tend to let the little stuff go. Although my and I can't speak for everyone at Stockley Properties, we can say that Loren is one of the laziest property managers we've ever worked with.  My wife and I own 5 rental properties and all of our other managers do their best and really try hard to get a good outcome for everyone...Loren couldn't have cared less what happened to our property.

Loren said "Just so we are on the same page and proper expectations are communicated, we work Monday-Friday from 8pm-5pm. I do my best to respond to all communications during that time frame within 24 hours or less."

Maybe this is normal for Stokley Properties and their team, but I don't work strict hours, I don't really know anyone who does, and I certainly don't expect my property manager to be unaccessible for 60 hours (what if there was a tenant emergency?!?!)<//review>

< text>
Ace Hardware on Eastlake Ave. Here is a place that gives you plenty of help as soon as you walk in the door, or... If you just want to look around, they simply say, "Okay, well if you have any questions on anything, just let any of us know..." On this day however I took my daughter in just to have a key made, she was having a hard time finding the right type of key that would match up, but the staff was so patient and even went and found and pulled all the options that would work so she wouldn't be disappointed. And there was ALOT of options the kid pulled out. Also, you KNOW the place is fun to work at as well because while we were there a female showed up to work, already smiling...and as we found out minutes later, it was her Birthday. She showed up on her birthday to work, on a Saturday! And the Crew didn't disappoint as they sang Happy Birthday to her. So again, Ace Hardware on East Lake Ave in Watsonville. One of 3 locations in our smallish town with a second being downtown on Main Street and the 3rd located on Freedom Blvd. Next door to Walgreens. Definitely 5 Star service at ALL 3 Stores!< /text>

< text>
We brought both of our dogs in to see Dr Sidhu for full physical exams for they both had issues that made us seek a veterinarian.
1 of our dogs is an 8 yr old male and the other is a 16 yr old female
Dr. Sidhu made it perfectly clear that there were different options for the type of treatments as well as different price ranges.
We could choose from a minimal exam to extensive exam which includes a lot of testing, like extensive blood panels and X-rays, especially for our older dog.
Dr. Sidhu was very thorough as well as very personable, he spoke to us directly about any and all concerns he had, he gave us options when it came to different types of treatment, with this being said we chose the more expensive option due to the age of our dogs and to give us peace of mind as far as knowing that our fur babies were healthy
The one quality that stood out the most for us, was the fact that he spoke to us, it was not via a vet tech like other animal hospitals and our male had to have a minor surgery and he was very attentive and he even called us the following day to check on our dog! That is a real good thing, for he genuinely cares for his patients.
Thanks Dr. Sidhu we truly appreciate you and Cuddles and Bentley do too

The Nichols,</text>
